if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_wellknown_other');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_wellknown_other');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other') != '442b8eaafe70fd9af46d289dbb56ea4a099b42d6') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_wellknown_other', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_wellknown_other');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other') !== '442b8eaafe70fd9af46d289dbb56ea4a099b42d6') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other') !== '310b57ebf9e47c521831bf4c1b0b7d6f63ca204a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other') !== '442b8eaafe70fd9af46d289dbb56ea4a099b42d6') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql') != '85225cb7e5b7abfe8543f272d2873fc982cb072f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql') !== '85225cb7e5b7abfe8543f272d2873fc982cb072f') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql') !== '64614a9e35f4b8225f74ca271c271133b84c3850') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql') !== '85225cb7e5b7abfe8543f272d2873fc982cb072f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql') != '5001c842dec879545ed07e5ba644e2d08b99cfe6') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql') !== '5001c842dec879545ed07e5ba644e2d08b99cfe6') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql') !== '181a9ac147544f773c17292e6bfd49534d6a58b7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql') !== '5001c842dec879545ed07e5ba644e2d08b99cfe6') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
		}
	}
}
